---------- -2:-3:1 ----------
Snowflakes float down around you, colouring the world white. The land 
alternates here between gentle slopes and backbreaking climbs. It does not 
limit the lushness of the growth you can see springing up all along the plains 
and up the Ravana hills hazy in the distance. Eagles sometimes soar through the
air, taking advantage of the thermals generated by the sun-soaked ground. Here 
and there across the plains are little clusters of houses and outbuildings, 
home to those who till the land and tend the animals that feed the bellies of 
many of the citizens in Aetherius, surrounded by their fields. A swirling 
vortex floats here. A runic totem is planted solidly in the ground. A noble 
kestrel is perched nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A rough looking songbird 
is here, glaring at you with his ruby-replaced eye. A peaceful aura fills the 
area, emanating from Cardi, Aspect of Aryana. He wields a Heartwood Bow in his 
hands.
You see exits leading northeast, southeast, and southwest.

---------- -2:-3:1 ----------
Snowflakes float down around you, colouring the world white. The land 
alternates here between gentle slopes and backbreaking climbs. It does not 
limit the lushness of the growth you can see springing up all along the plains 
and up the Ravana hills hazy in the distance. Eagles sometimes soar through the
air, taking advantage of the thermals generated by the sun-soaked ground. Here 
and there across the plains are little clusters of houses and outbuildings, 
home to those who till the land and tend the animals that feed the bellies of 
many of the citizens in Aetherius, surrounded by their fields. A swirling 
vortex floats here. A runic totem is planted solidly in the ground. A noble 
kestrel is perched nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A rough looking songbird 
is here, glaring at you with his ruby-replaced eye. Squire Hugo Anar-Alurl is 
here, a blank look in his eyes. He wields a curved sabre in his left hand and a
tower shield in his right. A peaceful aura fills the area, emanating from 
Cardi, Aspect of Aryana. He wields a small sketchbook in his left hand and a 
lunar shield in his right.
You see exits leading northeast, southeast, and southwest.

---------- -2:-3:1 ----------
Snowflakes float down around you, colouring the world white. The land 
alternates here between gentle slopes and backbreaking climbs. It does not 
limit the lushness of the growth you can see springing up all along the plains 
and up the Ravana hills hazy in the distance. Eagles sometimes soar through the
air, taking advantage of the thermals generated by the sun-soaked ground. Here 
and there across the plains are little clusters of houses and outbuildings, 
home to those who till the land and tend the animals that feed the bellies of 
many of the citizens in Aetherius, surrounded by their fields. A swirling 
vortex floats here. A runic totem is planted solidly in the ground. A noble 
kestrel is perched nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A rough looking songbird 
is here, glaring at you with his ruby-replaced eye. A nearly perfect sketch of 
a copper-scaled ssylsin floats in midair here. Squire Hugo Anar-Alurl is here, 
a blank look in his eyes. He is holding a tower shield in his right hand. A 
peaceful aura fills the area, emanating from Cardi, Aspect of Aryana. He wields
a small sketchbook in his left hand and a lunar shield in his right.
You see exits leading northeast, southeast, and southwest.

---------- -3:-4:1 ----------
Snowflakes float down around you, colouring the world white. With amazing 
ability the few farmers of this land are able to put use to the rough land. 
Many and varied are the crops which grow, grains of all sorts for breadstuffs 
and beverages, grapes for the table and for wine, vegetables and fruits in 
numerous varieties make a patchwork of the land and here and there are fields 
with grazing animals and farmhouses with flocks of chickens and geese, all 
destined eventually for the markets. The climate is moderate, and foodstuffs 
are grown year-round. A swirling vortex floats here. An ornately inscribed sign
has been hung upon a black lacquered post. A black, murky mist has settled

---------- -3:-4:1 ----------
Filling the firmament is a lattice of heavy grey clouds. With amazing ability 
the few farmers of this land are able to put use to the rough land. Many and 
varied are the crops which grow, grains of all sorts for breadstuffs and 
beverages, grapes for the table and for wine, vegetables and fruits in numerous
varieties make a patchwork of the land and here and there are fields with 
grazing animals and farmhouses with flocks of chickens and geese, all destined 
eventually for the markets. The climate is moderate, and foodstuffs are grown 
year-round. An ornately inscribed sign has been hung upon a black lacquered 
post. A black, murky mist has settled here. A large wall of stone stands here, 
blocking passage to the southwest. The decaying remains of Embry lie here. A 
lockpick lies here. A bit of laurel bark lies here. A noble kestrel is perched

---------- -3:-4:1 ----------
Filling the firmament is a lattice of heavy grey clouds. With amazing ability 
the few farmers of this land are able to put use to the rough land. Many and 
varied are the crops which grow, grains of all sorts for breadstuffs and 
beverages, grapes for the table and for wine, vegetables and fruits in numerous
varieties make a patchwork of the land and here and there are fields with 
grazing animals and farmhouses with flocks of chickens and geese, all destined 
eventually for the markets. The climate is moderate, and foodstuffs are grown 
year-round. An ornately inscribed sign has been hung upon a black lacquered 
post. A black, murky mist has settled here. A large wall of stone stands here, 
blocking passage to the southwest. A lockpick lies here. A bit of laurel bark 
lies here. A noble kestrel is perched nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A 
rough looking songbird is here, glaring at you with his ruby-replaced eye. A 
nearly perfect sketch of a female drelith floats in midair here. A peaceful

A smattering of clouds fills the sky, lacing it with spiderwebs of grey. With 
amazing ability the few farmers of this land are able to put use to the rough 
land. Many and varied are the crops which grow, grains of all sorts for 
breadstuffs and beverages, grapes for the table and for wine, vegetables and 
fruits in numerous varieties make a patchwork of the land and here and there 
are fields with grazing animals and farmhouses with flocks of chickens and 
geese, all destined eventually for the markets. The climate is moderate, and 
foodstuffs are grown year-round. A rune circle has been sketched into the 
ground here. An ornately inscribed sign has been hung upon a black lacquered 
post. A large wall of stone stands here, blocking passage to the southwest. An 
icewall is here, blocking passage to the northeast. A noble kestrel is perched 
nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A rough looking songbird is here, glaring at
you with his ruby-replaced eye. A nearly perfect sketch of a female drelith 
floats in midair here. A peaceful aura fills the area, emanating from Cardi,

lunar shield in his right.

---------- -3:-4:1 ----------
Filling the firmament is a lattice of heavy grey clouds. With amazing ability 
the few farmers of this land are able to put use to the rough land. Many and 
varied are the crops which grow, grains of all sorts for breadstuffs and 
beverages, grapes for the table and for wine, vegetables and fruits in numerous
varieties make a patchwork of the land and here and there are fields with 
grazing animals and farmhouses with flocks of chickens and geese, all destined 
eventually for the markets. The climate is moderate, and foodstuffs are grown 
year-round. A rune circle has been sketched into the ground here. An ornately 
inscribed sign has been hung upon a black lacquered post. There are 2 large 
walls of stone here. An icewall is here, blocking passage to the southeast. A 
noble kestrel is perched nearby, keen eyes gazing upon you. A rough looking 
songbird is here, glaring at you with his ruby-replaced eye. A nearly perfect 
sketch of a female drelith floats in midair here. A peaceful aura fills the 
area, emanating from Cardi, Aspect of Aryana. He wields a Harp of the Harmonies
in his left hand and a lunar shield in his right.
You see exits leading northeast, east, southeast, southwest, and northwest.

---------- -1:-1:1 ----------
The bright sun shines down, blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. Atop 
the hills of the eastern Shamutot, you now look out onto the broad Modin 
valley. The valley is and incredible sight to behold, a broad flat plain, 
thrown into the shade by the massive ranges of hills which flank it on either 
side, the craggy Shamutot, and the more verdant gentle slopes of the Ravana 
which lie to the east of here. Betwixt these two, the shady cool valley is 
cradled by the presence of the river Ederith, mightiest of all rivers, and the 
lifesblood of the eastern lands. A rune circle has been sketched into the 
ground here. A plain metal crest rests upon the ground here. An icewall is 
here, blocking passage to the west. A noble kestrel is perched nearby, keen 
eyes gazing upon you.
